			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading"><span dir="auto">List of <i>How I Met Your Mother</i> episodes</span></h1>
			<!-- /firstHeading -->
			<!-- bodyContent -->
			<div id="bodyContent">

<div style="display:none;" class="pef-notification-container historical">
	<div class="pef-notification">
		<div class="pef-icon pef-icon-checkmark">&#160;</div>
		<span></span>
	</div>
</div><p><i><b><a href="/wiki/How_I_Met_Your_Mother" title="How I Met Your Mother">How I Met Your Mother</a></b></i> (sometimes abbreviated as "HIMYM") is an American <a href="/wiki/Situation_comedy" title="Situation comedy" class="mw-redirect">situation comedy</a> (<a href="/wiki/Sitcom" title="Sitcom">sitcom</a>) that premiered on <a href="/wiki/CBS" title="CBS">CBS</a> on September 19, 2005. The show was created by <a href="/wiki/Craig_Thomas_(screenwriter)" title="Craig Thomas (screenwriter)">Craig Thomas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Carter_Bays" title="Carter Bays">Carter Bays</a>. <i>How I Met Your Mother</i> is framed by the year 2030, when Ted Mosby (voiced by <a href="/wiki/Bob_Saget" title="Bob Saget">Bob Saget</a>) gathers his daughter (<a href="/wiki/Lyndsy_Fonseca" title="Lyndsy Fonseca">Lyndsy Fonseca</a>) and son (<a href="/wiki/David_Henrie" title="David Henrie">David Henrie</a>) to tell them the story of how he met their mother. Flashback to where it begins in 2005 with <a href="/wiki/Ted_Mosby" title="Ted Mosby">Ted Mosby</a> (<a href="/wiki/Josh_Radnor" title="Josh Radnor">Josh Radnor</a>) as a single, 27-year-old architect living with his two best friends from <a href="/wiki/Wesleyan_University" title="Wesleyan University">Wesleyan University</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Eriksen" title="Marshall Eriksen">Marshall Eriksen</a> (<a href="/wiki/Jason_Segel" title="Jason Segel">Jason Segel</a>), a law student, and <a href="/wiki/Lily_Aldrin" title="Lily Aldrin">Lily Aldrin</a> (<a href="/wiki/Alyson_Hannigan" title="Alyson Hannigan">Alyson Hannigan</a>), a kindergarten teacher, who have been dating for almost nine years when Marshall proposes. Their engagement causes Ted to think about finding his own soul mate, much to the disgust of his friend <a href="/wiki/Barney_Stinson" title="Barney Stinson">Barney Stinson</a> (<a href="/wiki/Neil_Patrick_Harris" title="Neil Patrick Harris">Neil Patrick Harris</a>), a womanizer with an unnamed corporate job. And thus, Ted begins his search for his perfect mate, and meets <a href="/wiki/Robin_Scherbatsky" title="Robin Scherbatsky">Robin Scherbatsky</a> (<a href="/wiki/Cobie_Smulders" title="Cobie Smulders">Cobie Smulders</a>), whom he also befriends. The 100th episode of <i>How I Met Your Mother</i> aired on January 11, 2010. The series was renewed for a seventh and eighth season on March 1, 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-Season_8_0-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Season_8-0"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="editsection">[<a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_How_I_Met_Your_Mother_episodes&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Season 8: 2012">edit</a>]</span> <span class="mw-headline" id="Season_8:_2012">Season 8: 2012</span></h2>
<p>In March 2011, <i>How I Met Your Mother</i> was renewed for an eighth season. The season will premiere on September 24, 2012. <sup id="cite_ref-Season_8_0-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Season_8-0"><span>[</span>1<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
